//---------------------------------------------------------------------------
void __fastcall TSudoku::Timer4Timer(TObject *Sender)
{Hours->Visible=true;second->Visible=true;Ms->Visible=true;nut->Visible=true;Hm->Visible=true;hour->Visible=true;

if(1<=t&&t<=9){second->Caption="0"+IntToStr(t);}
else if(10<=t&&t<=59){second->Caption=IntToStr(t);}
else if(t==60){second->Caption="00"; r=StrToInt(nut->Caption); r++;
if(1<=r&&r<=9){nut->Caption="0"+IntToStr(r);}
else if(10<=r&&r<=59){nut->Caption=IntToStr(r);}
else if(r==60){nut->Caption="00";h=StrToInt(hour->Caption);h++;
if(1<=h&&h<=9){hour->Caption="0"+IntToStr(h);}
else if(10<=h&&h<=23){hour->Caption=IntToStr(h);}
else if(h==24){hour->Caption="00";d++;
if(d==1){Day->Visible=true;} else if(d>1){Day->Caption=IntToStr(d)+" Days";}}}}
}

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------
void __fastcall TSudoku::Image2Click(TObject *Sender)
{b=StrToInt(Label1->Caption);b+=10;
if(b>=10&&b<100){Label1->Caption="0"+IntToStr(b);}
else if(b==100){Label1->Caption=IntToStr(b);}
else if(b>100&&b<110){b-=100;Label1->Caption="00"+IntToStr(b);}
else if(b==110){b=10;Label1->Caption="0"+IntToStr(b);}
}
//---------------------------------------------------------------------------
void __fastcall TSudoku::Image3Click(TObject *Sender)
{b=StrToInt(Label1->Caption); b--;
if(b==99||b>=10){Label1->Caption="0"+IntToStr(b);}
else if(b==9||b>=1){Label1->Caption="00"+IntToStr(b);}
else {b=100;Label1->Caption=IntToStr(b);}
}

else if(b==10||b<100){Label1->Caption="0"+IntToStr(b);}
else if(b==100){Label1->Caption=IntToStr(b);}
else {b-=100;Label1->Caption="00"+IntToStr(b);}
}
//---------------------------------------------------------------------------
void __fastcall TSudoku::Image4Click(TObject *Sender)
{b=StrToInt(Label1->Caption);b-=10;
if(b>-10&&b<0){b+=100;Label1->Caption="0"+IntToStr(b);}
else if(b==0){b=100;Label1->Caption=IntToStr(b);}
else if(b<91&&b>9){Label1->Caption="0"+IntToStr(b);}
else if(b<=9&&b>=1){Label1->Caption="00"+IntToStr(b);}
}

void __fastcall TSudoku::Edit1KeyPress(TObject *Sender, char &Key)
{Edit1->Text="";
if(Edit1->ReadOnly==false)
{if(Key>='1'&&Key<='9'){kol=1;w=Key;Timer5->Enabled=true;}
else if(Key==VK_BACK){Edit1->Text="";w=' ';}
else  if(Key=='P'||Key=='p'||Key==27)
      {Sudoku->KeyPress(Key);Key=0;Edit1->Text=w;}
else {Key=0;Edit1->Text=w;}
}
else 
{if(Key=='P'||Key=='p'||Key==27)
      {Sudoku->KeyPress(Key);Key=0; Edit1->Text=key;}
else Edit1->Text=key;}
}

void __fastcall TSudoku::Timer5Timer(TObject *Sender)
{a[0][0]=Edit1->Text;a[0][4]=Edit11->Text;a[0][8]=Edit21->Text;a[4][0]=Edit31->Text;a[4][4]=Edit41->Text;a[4][8]=Edit51->Text;a[8][0]=Edit61->Text;a[8][4]=Edit71->Text;
 a[0][1]=Edit2->Text;a[0][5]=Edit12->Text;a[1][6]=Edit22->Text;a[4][1]=Edit32->Text;a[4][5]=Edit42->Text;a[5][6]=Edit52->Text;a[8][1]=Edit62->Text;a[8][5]=Edit72->Text;
 a[0][2]=Edit3->Text;a[1][3]=Edit13->Text;a[1][7]=Edit23->Text;a[4][2]=Edit33->Text;a[5][3]=Edit43->Text;a[5][7]=Edit53->Text;a[8][2]=Edit63->Text;a[6][6]=Edit73->Text;
 a[1][0]=Edit4->Text;a[1][4]=Edit14->Text;a[1][8]=Edit24->Text;a[5][0]=Edit34->Text;a[5][4]=Edit44->Text;a[5][8]=Edit54->Text;a[6][3]=Edit64->Text;a[6][7]=Edit74->Text;
 a[1][1]=Edit5->Text;a[1][5]=Edit15->Text;a[2][6]=Edit25->Text;a[5][1]=Edit35->Text;a[5][5]=Edit45->Text;a[6][0]=Edit55->Text;a[6][4]=Edit65->Text;a[6][8]=Edit75->Text;
 a[1][2]=Edit6->Text;a[2][3]=Edit16->Text;a[2][7]=Edit26->Text;a[5][2]=Edit36->Text;a[3][6]=Edit46->Text;a[6][1]=Edit56->Text;a[6][5]=Edit66->Text;a[7][6]=Edit76->Text;
 a[2][0]=Edit7->Text;a[2][4]=Edit17->Text;a[2][8]=Edit27->Text;a[3][3]=Edit37->Text;a[3][7]=Edit47->Text;a[6][2]=Edit57->Text;a[7][3]=Edit67->Text;a[7][7]=Edit77->Text;
 a[2][1]=Edit8->Text;a[2][5]=Edit18->Text;a[3][0]=Edit28->Text;a[3][4]=Edit38->Text;a[3][8]=Edit48->Text;a[7][0]=Edit58->Text;a[7][4]=Edit68->Text;a[7][8]=Edit78->Text;
 a[2][2]=Edit9->Text;a[0][6]=Edit19->Text;a[3][1]=Edit29->Text;a[3][5]=Edit39->Text;a[4][6]=Edit49->Text;a[7][1]=Edit59->Text;a[7][5]=Edit69->Text;a[8][6]=Edit79->Text;
 a[0][3]=Edit10->Text;a[0][7]=Edit20->Text;a[3][2]=Edit30->Text;a[4][3]=Edit40->Text;a[4][7]=Edit50->Text;a[7][2]=Edit60->Text;a[8][3]=Edit70->Text;a[8][7]=Edit80->Text;a[8][8]=Edit81->Text;
u=0;
switch(kol)
{case 1: for(i=1;i<9;i++)
         {if(a[0][0]!=a[0][i])
         u++;
         } if(u==8)
           {u=0;for(i=1;i<9;i++)
                {if(a[0][0]!=a[i][0])
                u++;
                } if(u==8)
                  {if(a[0][0]!=a[1][1])
                    {if(a[0][0]!=a[1][2])
                      {if(a[0][0]!=a[2][1])
                        {if(a[0][0]!=a[2][2])
                           {z[0][0]=1; Edit1->Font->Color=clLime;
                           }else {z[0][0]=0;Edit1->Font->Color=clRed;}
                        }else {z[0][0]=0;Edit1->Font->Color=clRed;}
                      }else {z[0][0]=0;Edit1->Font->Color=clRed;}
                    }else {z[0][0]=0;Edit1->Font->Color=clRed;}
                  }else {z[0][0]=0;Edit1->Font->Color=clRed;}
           }else {z[0][0]=0;Edit1->Font->Color=clRed;}break;
case 2: for(i=2;i<9;i++)
        {if(a[0][1]!=a[0][i])
        u++;}
        if(u==7)
        {u=0;for(i=1;i<9;i++)
             {if(a[0][1]!=a[i][1])
             u++;
             } if(u==8)
               {u=0;for(i=0;i<3;i++)
                  {if(a[0][1]!=a[i][0])
                  u++;
                  } if(u==3)
                    {u=0;if(a[0][1]!=a[1][2])
                         {if(a[0][1]!=a[2][2])
                         {z[0][1]=1; Edit2->Font->Color=clLime;
                         }else {z[0][1]=0;Edit2->Font->Color=clRed;}
                       }else {z[0][1]=0;Edit2->Font->Color=clRed;}
                   }else {z[0][1]=0;Edit2->Font->Color=clRed;}
              }else {z[0][1]=0;Edit2->Font->Color=clRed;}
        }else {z[0][1]=0; Edit2->Font->Color=clRed;}
        break;
case 3: for(i=3;i<9;i++)
        {if(a[0][2]!=a[0][i])
        u++;
        } if(u==6)
        {u=0;for(i=1;i<9;i++)
             {if(a[0][2]!=a[i][2])
             u++;
             } if(u==8)
               {u=0;for(i=0;i<3;i++)
                    for(j=0;j<2;j++)
                    if(a[0][2]!=a[i][j])
                    {u++;
                    } if(u==6)
                      {z[0][2]=1; Edit3->Font->Color=clLime;
                      }else {z[0][0]=0;Edit3->Font->Color=clRed;}
               }else {z[0][2]=0;Edit3->Font->Color=clRed;}
        }else {z[0][2]=0;Edit3->Font->Color=clRed;}
        break;
case 4: for(i=1;i<9;i++)
        {if(a[1][0]!=a[1][i])
        u++;
        } if(u==8)
            {u=0; for(i=3;i<9;i++)
                  {if(a[1][0]!=a[i][0])
                  u++;
                  } if(u==6)
                  {u=0;for(i=0;i<3;i+=2)
                       for(j=0;j<3;j++)
                       {if(a[1][0]!=a[i][j])
                       u++;
                       }
                       if(u==6)
                       {z[1][0]=1;Edit4->Font->Color=clLime;
                       }else {z[1][0]=0;Edit4->Font->Color=clRed;}
                  }else {z[1][0]=0;Edit4->Font->Color=clRed;}
            }else {z[1][0]=0; Edit4->Font->Color=clRed;}
        break;
case 5: for(i=2;i<9;i++)
        {if(a[1][1]!=a[1][i])
        u++;
        } if(u==7)
          {u=0;for(i=3;i<9;i++)
               {if(a[1][1]!=a[i][1])
               u++;

                   }else {z[8][8]=0; Edit81->Font->Color=clRed;}
           }else {z[8][8]=0; Edit81->Font->Color=clRed;}
}Button7->Visible=false;
 }
